More skills and levels are unlocked as you level up further.\n\n<color\=#FFD145>Inspiration Reset</color>\nYou can reset your skill tree by spending Konpaku Gem, which will return all the Inspiration Points you have used.

当停留在<color\=#ff3b37>事件地块</color>上时，会触发随机事件。\n根据玩家选择选项的不同，可能会触发不同的效果：\n如获取物品、获得有利的正面BUFF。=When stopping at an <color\=#ff3b37>Event Tile</color>, activate random events.\nActivate different effects based on your choice.

命运骰子争霸赛·建筑格=Dice Championship·Building Tiles
当停留在<color\=#ff3b37>建筑地块</color>上时，可以消耗资金<color\=#ff3b37>购买</color>该建筑；\n经过已购买的建筑时，可以获取<color\=#ff3b37>资金收益</color>。\n停留在已购买建筑地块上时，可以<color\=#ff3b37>升级</color>该建筑；\n升级后，该建筑产生的资金收益也会得到提升。=When stopping at a <color\=#ff3b37>Building Tile</color>, you can spend Funds to <color\=#ff3b37>purchase</color> that Building;\nWhen passing through a purchased Building, you can obatin <color\=#ff3b37>Funds</color>.\nWhen stopping at a purchased Building Tile, you can <color\=#ff3b37>level up</color> that Building\n; After levelled, increase that Building's Fund Gain.
部分建筑会由多个连续地块组成。\n停留在任一地块上时，都可以触发该建筑的效果。\n在这些地块内部移动时，仅可<color\=#ff3b37>触发一次</color>建筑效果。=Cetain Buildings consist of multiple consecutive Tiles. \nWhen stopping at any Tiles, you can activate that Building's effect.\nWhen moving within those Tiles, you can only activate the Building effect <color\=#ff3b37>once</color>.
可以随时查看当前的建筑收购情况。\n在<color\=#ff3b37>建筑列表</color>中，罗列了包含的全部建筑的详细资讯。=You can check the <color\=#ff3b37>Building List</color> for details on all Buildings.

委托类型=Task Types
「<color\=#ff3b37>限定</color>」委托，在满足特定条件后出现。\n「<color\=#ff3b37>每周、每日</color>」委托，周期内仅刷新一个。\n「<color\=#ff3b37>常规</color>」委托，完成后自动刷新。=<size\=25>[<color\=#ff3b37>Limited</color>] Tasks, appear after fulfilling certain conditions. \n[<color\=#ff3b37>Weekly, Daily</color>] Tasks, with 1 refresh per week/ day. \n[<color\=#ff3b37>Standard</color>] Tasks, auto refresh on completion.</size>
委托刷新=Tasks Refresh
可以一次性刷新所有未派遣的「<color\=#ff3b37>非限定</color>」委托。\n刷新需要消耗「委托刷新券」。\n<color\=#ff3b37>每日首次刷新免费</color>=<size\=28>You can refresh all undispatched [<color\=#ff3b37>Non-limited</color>] Tasks. \nRefreshing requires a [Task Refresh Ticket].\n<color\=#ff3b37>The first refresh each day is free.</color></size>

完成委托后，会累计委托经验。\n随委托等级提升：\n增加<color\=#ff3b37>同时可接</color>委托任务数量；\n增加<color\=#ff3b37>同时刷出</color>的「常规」委托数量。=<size\=26>Gain Task EXP after completing Tasks. \nBased on your Tasks Level: \nIncrease the number of <color\=#ff3b37>active</color> Tasks: \nIncrease the number of <color\=#ff3b37>refreshes</color> on [Standard] Tasks.</size>
